<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Company reaffirms 2013 Organic Net Revenue growth outlook at the low end </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:13%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">of 5 &#150; 7% range and raises Operating EPS guidance to $1.55 &#150; $1.60 </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#150; May&nbsp;7, 2013 &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) today reported first quarter 2013 results.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%;padding-bottom:0px; "><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Our first quarter results were in line with the expectations we outlined earlier this year as we work
through some near-term headwinds,&#148; said Irene Rosenfeld, Chairman and CEO. &#147;Although we&#146;re not satisfied that our top-line growth remained below our long-term target, our results show that we&#146;ve built solid underlying
momentum.&nbsp;And I&#146;m confident that we&#146;ll deliver our 2013 commitments as we continue to leverage our advantaged category mix, leading market positions and strong geographic footprint, particularly in emerging markets</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">2</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Net revenues were $8.7 billion, up 0.9 percent. Organic Net Revenues increased 3.8 percent, including solid contributions from higher volume/mix of 2.5 percentage points and favorable pricing of 1.3 percentage
points. The pass-through of lower coffee commodity costs tempered the company&#146;s overall top-line growth by 1.3 percentage points. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%;padding-bottom:0px; "><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Revenues from emerging markets accelerated sequentially, up 9.3 percent, led by double-digit gains in China, Brazil and India, and continued improvement in Russia. Developed markets</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">3</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> grew 0.4 percent, with growth in North America partially offset by the impact of lower
coffee pricing in Europe and continued gum weakness. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Power Brands grew 7.5 percent, nearly double the company rate. <I>Tuc/Club Social,
Chips Ahoy!</I>, <I>Barni</I> and <I>Oreo</I> biscuits, <I>Milka</I>, <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk </I>and <I>Lacta</I> chocolate, <I>Halls</I> candy, <I>Stride</I> gum and <I>Tang</I> beverages each posted strong increases. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%;padding-bottom:0px; "><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Gross profit was $3.2 billion, up 1.5 percent, while gross profit margin was 37.1 percent. Adjusted Gross Profit</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> increased 3.9 percent on a constant currency basis, driven by strong volume/mix gains.
Pricing fully offset higher input costs. Adjusted Gross Profit margin was flat to prior year. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">1 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Operating income was $0.8 billion, down 7.6 percent, while operating income margin was 9.5 percent.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%;padding-bottom:0px; "><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Operating Income</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> decreased 4.0 percent on a constant currency basis, and included a negative 3.4 percentage point impact from previously disclosed
prior year one-time items.</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">4</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> Excluding these items, gross profit gains were
more than offset by higher SG&amp;A predominately in emerging markets, including increased investments in sales capabilities, route-to-market expansion as well as advertising and consumer support. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%;padding-bottom:0px; "><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Operating Income margin was 10.3 percent, down 1.6 percentage points, including the negative impacts of 0.6
percentage points due to the devaluation of net monetary assets in Venezuela and 0.4 percentage points from prior year one-time
items.</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">4</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"> </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Diluted EPS was $0.32. Operating EPS was $0.34, including a negative $0.04 impact from currency. On a constant currency basis, Operating EPS
increased 22.6 percent, reflecting a positive $0.09 impact of lower taxes, primarily from discrete items. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Strong Momentum in Latin America Led by
Brazil </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Latin America delivered strong top-line growth driven by a resurgence in Brazil and solid performance in other key markets in
the region. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Net revenues increased 2.0 percent. Organic Net Revenues grew 12.6 percent, with contributions from both higher pricing and
volume/mix. Brazil increased mid-teens with double-digit volume/mix gains and higher pricing. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Power Brands grew 12.3 percent, led by
<I>Club Social </I>and <I>Oreo</I> biscuits, <I>Lacta</I> chocolate and <I>Halls</I> candy. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Segment operating income decreased 43.6
percent. Segment operating income margin decreased 5.3 percentage points to 6.6 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Segment Operating Income was flat
versus prior year on a constant currency basis. Higher gross profit was offset by higher overheads, including increased investments in sales capabilities and route-to-market expansion. Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin was 6.9 percent, down
5.7 percentage points primarily due to negative impacts from the devaluation of the Venezuelan bolivar. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Emerging Markets in Asia Pacific Drove Solid
Top-line Growth </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Asia Pacific delivered strong emerging markets performance despite capacity constraints in India, while the
region&#146;s developed markets restrained overall growth. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Net revenues increased 3.6 percent. Organic Net Revenues grew 5.8 percent,
driven by both higher volume/mix and pricing. Organic Net Revenues for the region&#146;s emerging markets grew double digits, led by China, India and the Philippines. Developed markets in the region declined low single digits, largely due to gum
weakness in Japan. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">2 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Power Brands grew very strongly, up 20.3 percent, led by <I>Oreo</I> and <I>Chips Ahoy! </I>biscuits,
<I>Cadbury Dairy Milk </I>chocolate, <I>Halls</I> candy, <I>Stride</I> gum and <I>Tang</I> beverages. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Segment operating income
increased 6.8 percent. Segment operating income margin increased 0.4 percentage points to 13.8 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Segment Operating
Income increased 4.8 percent on a constant currency basis, including a positive 10.1 percentage point impact from cycling of a prior year asset impairment charge. Excluding this impact, higher gross profit was more than offset by higher overheads,
including increased investments in sales capabilities and route-to-market expansion, as well as increased A&amp;C support. Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin decreased 0.1 percentage point to 14.1 percent. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Strong Volume/Mix Growth for EEMEA </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Strong
volume/mix gains across the region, as well as continued sequential improvement in Russia, drove solid top-line growth for the Eastern Europe, Middle East and Africa region. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Net revenues increased 1.6 percent. Organic Net Revenues grew 4.0 percent, as strong volume/mix gains were partially offset by lower pricing. Russia continued to improve sequentially with organic growth in the low
single digits behind strong volume/mix performance, partially offset by significantly lower pricing in coffee and chocolate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Power
Brands grew 8.1 percent, led by <I>Oreo and Barni </I>biscuits, <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk </I>chocolate, <I>Halls</I> candy, and <I>Jacobs</I> and <I>Tang</I> beverages. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Segment operating income decreased 55.8 percent. Segment operating income margin decreased 9.2 percentage points to 7.1 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Segment Operating Income decreased 46.5 percent on a constant currency basis, including a negative 38.2 percentage point impact from cycling the prior year&#146;s gain on the sale of property in Russia.
Excluding this impact, higher gross profit was more than offset by higher overheads, including increased investments in sales capabilities and route-to-market expansion, as well as increased A&amp;C support. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin was 8.5 percent, down 8.9 percentage points, including a negative 6.7 percentage point impact from cycling
the prior year&#146;s gain on the sale of property in Russia. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Steady Results in Europe </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Europe delivered solid volume/mix gains in a difficult economic environment, while a significant headwind from coffee pricing tempered the top line
overall. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Net revenues decreased 1.0 percent. Organic Net Revenues increased 0.1 percent, as volume/mix gains, particularly in chocolate
and biscuits, were mostly offset by significant coffee pricing impacts. Lower coffee revenues negatively affected the region&#146;s growth by more than 2 percentage points. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">3 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Power Brands grew 2.8 percent, led by <I>Oreo, belVita</I> and chocobakery biscuits, <I>Milka</I>
chocolate, <I>Halls</I> candy and <I>Tassimo</I> beverages. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Segment operating income decreased 4.7 percent. Segment operating income
margin decreased 0.5 percentage points to 11.7 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Segment Operating Income was essentially flat to prior year on a
constant currency basis. Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin held steady at 12.6 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Solid Revenue Growth in North America </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Strong biscuit performance in the U.S. and a return to growth in Canada drove a solid increase in Organic Net Revenue. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Net revenues increased 1.5 percent. Organic Net Revenues increased 2.4 percent, with contributions from both pricing and volume/mix. Biscuits in
the U.S. grew mid-single digits for the seventh consecutive quarter. Canada performance improved with the resolution of its spin-related execution issues. Weak gum results, however, drove a high-single-digit decline in gum and candy, tempering the
region&#146;s overall growth. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Power Brands grew 5.6 percent, led by biscuits, primarily<I> Chips Ahoy! </I>and<I> Oreo</I>. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Segment operating income increased 14.9 percent. Segment operating income margin increased 1.2 percentage points to 10.3 percent. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Adjusted Segment Operating Income was essentially flat to prior year on a constant currency basis. Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin was
11.6 percent, down 0.4 percentage points as lower gross margin, pressured by weak gum results, more than offset benefits from overhead leverage. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Outlook </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%;padding-bottom:0px; "><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Lower
coffee pricing and capacity constraints in certain markets are expected to continue to temper top-line growth in the second quarter,&#148; said David Brearton, Executive Vice President and CFO.&nbsp;&#147;However, we expect a strong rebound in the
back half of the year, and we remain on track to deliver Organic Net Revenue growth at the low end of our long-term growth target of 5 to 7 percent. We&#146;re also raising our Operating EPS outlook to $1.55 to $1.60</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">5</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">, as we flow through a portion of the benefit from discrete tax items.&#148; </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">4 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Conference Call </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Mondel&#275;z International will host a conference call for investors with accompanying slides to review its results at 5 p.m. ET today. Access to a live audio webcast with accompanying slides and a replay of the
event will be available at <U>www.mondelezinternational.com/Investor</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) is a global snacking powerhouse, with 2012 revenue of $35 billion. Creating delicious moments of
joy in 165 countries, Mondel&#275;z International is a world leader in chocolate, biscuits, gum, candy, coffee and powdered beverages, with billion-dollar brands such as <I>Cadbury</I>,<I> Cadbury Dairy Milk</I> and <I>Milka</I> chocolate,
<I>Jacobs</I> coffee, <I>LU</I>, <I>Nabisco</I> and <I>Oreo</I> biscuits, <I>Tang</I> powdered beverages and <I>Trident</I> gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, NASDAQ 100 and Dow Jones
Sustainability Index. Visit <U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U> and <U>www.facebook.com/mondelezinternational</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:8px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000;width:10%">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">With the 2013 change in reporting structure, the company is introducing the emerging markets metric to illustrate performance where opportunities for growth
exist due to favorable demographic trends, rising per capita incomes, improving infrastructures and other factors that have the potential to significantly drive GDP growth. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Emerging markets, which accounted for nearly 40 percent of the company&#146;s revenues in 2012, consist of the Latin America and Eastern Europe, Middle East and Africa regions in
their entirety; the Asia Pacific region, excluding Australia, New Zealand and Japan; and the following countries from the Europe region: Poland, Czech&nbsp;&amp; Slovak Republics, Hungary, Bulgaria, Romania, the Baltics and the East Adriatic
countries. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">3.</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">The company considers all markets not included in the emerging markets definition to be developed markets. Developed markets include the entire North America
region, the Europe region, excluding the countries included in the emerging markets definition, and Australia, New Zealand and Japan from the Asia Pacific region. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Includes the prior year impacts of gain on sale of property in Russia and an asset impairment charge. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Operating EPS guidance of $1.55-$1.60 is based on 2012 average currency rates and includes the estimated impact of the write-down of the net monetary assets and
the translation of operating income for the company&#146;s Venezuelan business stemming from that government&#146;s decision to devalue its currency to a fixed rate of 6.30/$US on February&nbsp;8, 2013. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">This press release contains a number of forward-looking statements. Words, and variations of words, such as &#147;reaffirms,&#148; &#147;expect,&#148; &#147;on track,&#148; &#147;deliver,&#148; &#147;outlook,&#148;
&#147;guidance,&#148; &#147;momentum&#148; and similar expressions are intended to identify our forward-looking statements, including, but not limited to, statements about: 2013 guidance; delivering our 2013 commitments; leveraging our advantaged
category mix, leading market positions and strong geographic footprint; and our Outlook, in particular, the impacts of lower coffee pricing and capacity constraints, a strong rebound in the back half of 2013, 2013 Organic Net Revenue growth and
Operating EPS. These forward-looking statements are subject to a number of risks and uncertainties, many of which are beyond our control, which could cause our actual results to differ materially from those indicated in our forward-looking
statements. Such factors include, but are not limited to, continued volatility of commodity and other input costs, pricing actions, continued global economic weakness, risks from operating globally and tax law changes. Please also see our risk
factors, as they may be amended from time to time, set forth in our filings with the SEC, including our most recently filed Annual Report on Form 10-K. Mondel&#275;z International disclaims and does not undertake any obligation to update or revise
any forward-looking statement in this press release, except as required by applicable law or regulation. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Non-GAAP Financial Measures </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">The company reports its financial results in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#147;GAAP&#148;). We
use certain non-GAAP financial measures to budget, make operating and strategic decisions and evaluate our performance. We disclose non-GAAP financial measures so that you have the same financial data that we use to assist you in making comparisons
to our historical operating results and analyzing our underlying performance. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Our non-GAAP financial measures and corresponding metrics
reflect how we evaluate our operating results currently and provide improved comparability of operating results. As new events or circumstances arise, these definitions could change over time: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Organic Net Revenues&#148; which is defined as net revenues excluding the impacts of acquisitions, divestitures (including businesses under a sales
agreement), Integration Program costs, accounting calendar changes and foreign currency rate fluctuations. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">6 </FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Adjusted Gross Profit&#148; which is defined as gross profit excluding the impact of pension costs related to obligations transferred in the Spin-Off, the
2012-2014 Restructuring Program, the Integration Program and the operating results of divestitures (including businesses under a sales agreement). We also evaluate growth in our Adjusted Gross Profit on a constant currency basis.
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Adjusted Operating Income and Adjusted Segment Operating Income&#148; which are defined as operating income (or segment operating income) excluding the
impact of Spin-Off Costs, pension costs related to the obligations transferred in the Spin-Off, the 2012-2014 Restructuring Program, the Integration Program, gains / losses from divestitures or acquisitions, acquisition-related costs and the
operating results of divestitures (including businesses under a sales agreement). We also evaluate growth in our Adjusted Operating Income and Adjusted Segment Operating Income on a constant currency basis. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#147;Operating EPS&#148; which is defined as diluted EPS attributable to Mondel&#275;z International from continuing operations excluding the impact of Spin-Off
Costs, pension costs related to the obligations transferred in the Spin-Off, the 2012-2014 Restructuring Program, the Integration Program, gains / losses from divestitures or acquisitions, acquisition-related costs and net earnings from divestitures
(including businesses under a sales agreement), and including an interest expense adjustment related to the Spin-Off transaction. We also evaluate growth in our Operating EPS on a constant currency basis. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">We believe that the presentation of these non-GAAP financial measures, when considered together with our U.S. GAAP financial measures and the
reconciliations to the corresponding U.S. GAAP financial measures, provides you with a more complete understanding of the factors and trends affecting our business than could be obtained absent these disclosures. In addition, the non-GAAP measures
the company is using may differ from non-GAAP measures used by other companies. Because GAAP financial measures on a forward-looking basis are neither accessible nor deemed to be significantly different from the non-GAAP financial measures, and
reconciling information is not available without unreasonable effort, with regard to the non-GAAP financial measures in the company&#146;s Outlook, the company has not provided that information. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">See the attached schedules for supplemental financial data and corresponding reconciliations of the non-GAAP financial measures referred to above
to the most comparable GAAP financial measures for the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2013 and 2012. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">7 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Segment Operating Income </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Management uses segment operating income to evaluate segment performance and allocate resources. The company believes it is appropriate to disclose this measure to help investors analyze segment performance and
trends. Segment operating income excludes unrealized gains and losses on hedging activities (which are a component of cost of sales), general corporate expenses (which are a component of selling, general and administrative expenses), amortization of
intangibles, gains and losses from divestitures and acquisitions, and acquisition-related costs (which are a component of selling, general and administrative expenses) for all periods presented. The company excludes the unrealized gains and losses
on hedging activities from segment operating income in order to provide better transparency of our segment operating results. Once realized, the gains and losses on hedging activities are recorded within segment operating results. We exclude general
corporate expenses, amortization of intangibles, gains and losses on divestitures and acquisitions and acquisition-related costs from segment operating income in order to provide better transparency of our segment operating results. </FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Spin-Off Costs represent transaction and transition costs associated with preparing the businesses for independent operations consisting primarily of financial
advisory fees, legal fees, accounting fees, tax services and information systems infrastructure duplication, and financing and related costs to redistribute debt and secure investment grade ratings for both the Kraft Foods Group business and the
Mondel&#275;z International business. Spin-Off related adjustments include the pension adjustment defined as the estimated benefit plan expense associated with certain benefit plan obligations transferred to Kraft Foods Group in the Spin-Off.

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(2)</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2"></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Spin-Off Costs represent transaction and transition costs associated with preparing the businesses for independent operations consisting primarily of financial
advisory fees, legal fees, accounting fees, tax services and information systems infrastructure duplication, and financing and related costs to redistribute debt and secure investment grade ratings for both the Kraft Foods Group business and the
Mondel&#275;z International business. Spin-Off related adjustments include: (a)&nbsp;a pension adjustment defined as the estimated benefit plan expense associated with certain benefit plan obligations transferred to Kraft Foods Group in the
Spin-Off; and (b)&nbsp;an interest adjustment defined as the interest expense associated with the assumed reduction of the $6 billion of our debt on January&nbsp;1, 2012, from the utilization of funds received from Kraft Foods Group in 2012 in
connection with our Spin-Off capitalization plan. Note during the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2012, a portion of the $6 billion of debt was retired. As such, we adjusted interest expense during this period as if this debt had been paid on
January&nbsp;1, 2012 to ensure consistency of our assumption and related results. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Restructuring Program costs represent restructuring and related implementation costs reflecting primarily severance, asset disposals and other
manufacturing-related costs. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">On February&nbsp;22, 2013, the company acquired the remaining interest in a biscuit operation in Morocco, which is now a wholly-owned subsidiary within the EEMEA
segment. A pre-tax gain of $22 million was recorded in connection with the acquisition. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(1)</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Integration Program costs are defined as the costs associated with combining the Mondel&#275;z International and Cadbury businesses, and are separate from those

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(2)</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Spin-Off Costs represent transaction and transition costs associated with preparing the businesses for independent operations consisting primarily of financial
advisory fees, legal fees, accounting fees, tax services and information systems infrastructure duplication, and financing and related costs to redistribute debt and secure investment grade ratings for both the Kraft Foods Group business and the
Mondel&#275;z International business. Spin-Off related adjustments include the pension adjustment defined as the estimated benefit plan expense associated with certain benefit plan obligations transferred to Kraft Foods Group in the Spin-Off.
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(3)</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Restructuring Program costs represent restructuring and related implementation costs reflecting primarily severance, asset disposals and other
manufacturing-related costs. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">Includes divestitures and businesses for which Mondel&#275;z International has entered into a sales agreement. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(5)</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1">On February&nbsp;22, 2013, the company acquired the remaining interest in a biscuit operation in Morocco, which is now a wholly-owned subsidiary within the EEMEA
segment. A pre-tax gain of $22 million was recorded in connection with the acquisition. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">13 </FONT></P>

advisory fees, legal fees, accounting fees, tax services and information systems infrastructure duplication, and financing and related costs to redistribute debt and secure investment grade ratings for both the Kraft Foods Group business and the
Mondel&#275;z International business. Spin-Off related adjustments include the pension adjustment defined as the estimated benefit plan expense associated with certain benefit plan obligations transferred to Kraft Foods Group in the Spin-Off.

million, or $40 million after-tax for the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2012. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="2">Spin-Off Costs represent transaction and transition costs associated with preparing the businesses for independent operations consisting primarily of financial
advisory fees, legal fees, accounting fees, tax services and information systems infrastructure duplication, and financing and related costs to redistribute debt and secure investment grade ratings for both the Kraft Foods Group business and the
Mondel&#275;z International business. Spin-Off Costs for the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2013 were $9 million, or $5 million after-tax, as compared to $173 million or $113 million after-tax for the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2012.

transferred to Kraft Foods Group in the Spin-Off; and (b)&nbsp;interest adjustment defined as the interest expense associated with the assumed reduction of the $6 billion of our debt on January&nbsp;1, 2012, from the utilization of funds received
from Kraft Foods Group in 2012 in connection with our Spin-Off capitalization plan. Note during the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2012, a portion of the $6 billion of debt was retired. As such, we adjusted interest expense during this period as if
this debt had been paid on January&nbsp;1, 2012 to ensure consistency of our assumption and related results. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

segment. A pre-tax gain of $22 million was recorded in connection with the acquisition. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
